    level_up: \'‚¨ÜÔ∏è\',\n      streak_milestone: \'üî•\',\n      challenge: \'‚úÖ\',\n      major_milestone: \'üéâ\'\n    };\n    return icons[type] || \'‚≠ê\';\n  }\n\n  triggerCelebration(tier) [\'#C0C0C0\', \'#E8E8E8\'],\n        gold: [\'#FFD700\', \'#FFA500\'],\n        diamond: [\'#B9F2FF\', \'#00CED1\'],\n        level_up: [\'#4A90E2\', \'#9B59B6\', \'#E74C3C\']\n      };\n      \n });\n    }\n  }\n\n  onAchievement(callback) {\n    this.listeners.push(callback);\n  }\n\n  shuffleArray(array) {\n    const shuffled = [...array];\n    for (let i = shuffled.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {\n      const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));\n      [shuffled[i], shuffled[j]] = [shuffled[j], shuffled[i]];\n    }\n    return shuffled;\n  }\n\n  // Public API methods\n  getProgress() {\n    return {\n      ...this.userProgress,\n      nextLevel: this.getNextLevel(),\n      progressToNextLevel: this.getProgressToNextLevel()\n    };\n  }\n\n  getNextLevel() {\n    const levels = this.achievements.level_system.levels;\n    const currentLevel = this.userProgress.level;\n    return levels.find(l => l.level === currentLevel + 1);\n  }\n\n  getProgressToNextLevel() {\n    const nextLevel = this.getNextLevel();\n    if (!nextLevel) return 100; // Max level\n    \n    const currentPoints = this.userProgress.points;\n    const currentLevelPoints = this.achievements.level_system.levels\n      .find(l => l.level === this.userProgress.level).points_required;\n    const nextLevelPoints = nextLevel.points_required;\n    \n    const progress = ((currentPoints - currentLevelPoints) / (nextLevelPoints - currentLevelPoints)) * 100;\n    return Math.min(100, Math.max(0, progress));\n  }\n\n  getUnlockedAchievements() {\n    const unlocked = [];\n    const categories = this.achievements.achievement_categories;\n    \n    for (const [categoryKey, category] of Object.entries(categories)) {\n      for (const achievement of category.achievements) {\n        if (this.userProgress.unlockedAchievements.includes(achievement.id)) {\n          unlocked.push({\n            ...achievement,\n            category: category.name,\n            categoryIcon: category.icon\n          });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    \n    return unlocked;\n  }\n\n  getDailyChallenges() {\n    return this.userProgress.dailyChallenges;\n  }\n\n  getStreaks() {\n    return this.userProgress.streaks;\n  }\n\n  getBadges() {\n    return this.userProgress.badges.map(badgeId => {\n      return {\n        id: badgeId,\n        ...this.achievements.badges[badgeId]\n      };\n    });\n  }\n\n  isFeatureUnlocked(featureName) {\n    return this.userProgress.unlockedFeatures?.includes(featureName) || false;\n  }\n\n  isPersonaUnlocked(personaName) {\n    return this.userProgress.unlockedPersonas?.includes(personaName) || false;\n  }\n\n  getActiveBoosts() {\n    if (!this.userProgress.activeBoosts) return [];\n    \n    const now = new Date();\n    return this.userProgress.activeBoosts.filter(boost => {\n      return new Date(boost.endDate) > now;\n    });\n  }\n\n  getTotalBoostPercentage() {\n    const activeBoosts = this.getActiveBoosts();\n    return activeBoosts.reduce((total, boost) => total + boost.percentage, 0);\n  }\n}\n\n// Export for use in other modules\nif (typeof module !== \'undefined\' && module.exports) {\n  module.exports = AchievementTracker;\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

    document.getElementById(\'momentumScore\').textContent = snapshot.momentum + \'%\';\n      document.getElementById(\'completionScore\').textContent = snapshot.completionPercentage + \'%\';\n\n ${stars.split(\'\').map(s => `<span class="star ${s === \'‚òÜ\' ? \'empty\' : \'\'}">${s}</span>`).join(\'\')}\n          </div>\n        `;\n        \n        list.appendChild(item);\n      });\n    }\n\n    function renderInsights() {\n      const insights = realityTracker.getManifestationInsights();\n      if (!insights) return;\n\n      const section = document.getElementById(id);\n        container.querySelectorAll(\'.tag\').forEach(tag => tag.remove());\n      });\n    }\n\n    function setupTagInput(inputId, containerId, tagKey) {\n      const input = document.getElementById(inputId);\n      const container = document.getElementById(containerId);\n\n      input.addEventListener(\'keypress\', (e) => {\n        if (e.key === \'Enter\' && input.value.trim()) {\n          e.preventDefault();\n          addTag(input.value.trim(), container, tagKey);\n          input.value = \'\';\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    function addTag(text, container, tagKey) {\n      tags[tagKey].push(text);\n\n      const tag = document.createElement(\'div\');\n      tag.className = \'tag\';\n      tag.innerHTML = `\n        <span>${text}</span>\n        <span class="tag-remove" onclick="removeTag(this, \'${tagKey}\', \'${text}\')">√ó</span>\n      `;\n\n      const input = container.querySelector(\'.tag-input\');\n      container.insertBefore(tag, input);\n    }\n\n    function removeTag(element, tagKey, text) {\n      const index = tags[tagKey].indexOf(text);\n      if (index > -1) {\n        tags[tagKey].splice(index, 1);\n      }\n      element.parentElement.remove();\n    }\n\n    function setupSlider(sliderId, valueId) {\n      const slider = document.getElementById(sliderId);\n      const valueDisplay = document.getElementById(valueId);\n\n      slider.addEventListener(\'input\', () => {\n        valueDisplay.textContent = slider.value;\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Initialize on load\n    init();\n {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="sw.js">\n// Service Worker for Quantum Council PWA\nconst CACHE_NAME = \'quantum-council-v1\';\nconst STATIC_CACHE = \'quantum-static-v1\';\n\n// Files to cache for offline functionality\nconst STATIC_FILES = [\n  \'/\',\n  \'/index.html\',\n  \'/manifest.json\',\n  \'/sw.js\',\n  \'https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap\'\n];\n\n// Install event - cache static files\nself.addEventListener(\'install\', event => {\n  console.log(\'[SW] Installing service worker...\');\n  event.waitUntil(\n    caches.open(STATIC_CACHE)\n      .then(cache => {\n        console.log(\'[SW] Caching static files\');\n        return cache.addAll(STATIC_FILES);\n      })\n      .then(() => self.skipWaiting())\n  );\n});\n\n// Activate event - clean up old caches\nself.addEventListener(\'activate\', event => {\n  console.log(\'[SW] Activating service worker...\');\n  event.waitUntil(\n    caches.keys()\n      .then(cacheNames => {\n        return Promise.all(\n          cacheNames\n            .filter(cacheName => \n              cacheName !== STATIC_CACHE && \n              cacheName !== CACHE_NAME\n            )\n            .map(cacheName => {\n              console.log(\'[SW] Deleting old cache:\', cacheName);\n              return caches.delete(cacheName);\n            })\n        );\n      })\n      .then(() => self.clients.claim())\n  );\n});\n\n// Fetch event - serve from cache, fallback to network\nself.addEventListener(\'fetch\', event => {\n  const { request } = event;\n  const url = new URL(request.url);\n\n  // Skip caching for non-GET requests\n  if (request.method !== \'GET\') return;\n\n  // Skip caching for external resources (except fonts)\n  if (!url.origin.includes(self.location.origin) && !url.hostname.includes(\'fonts.googleapis.com\')) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  event.respondWith(\n    caches.match(request)\n      .then(cached => {\n        // Serve from cache if available\n        if (cached) {\n          return cached;\n        }\n\n        // Otherwise fetch from network\n        return fetch(request)\n          .then(response => {\n            // Don\'t cache non-successful responses\n            if (!response || response.status !== 200 || response.type !== \'basic\') {\n              return response;\n            }\n\n            // Clone the response since it can only be used once\n            const responseToCache = response.clone();\n\n            // Cache the fetched resource\n            caches.open(CACHE_NAME)\n              .then(cache => {\n                cache.put(request, responseToCache);\n              });\n\n            return response;\n          })\n          .catch(() => {\n            // Return offline page for HTML requests\n            if (request.headers.get(\'accept\').includes(\'text/html\')) {\n              return new Response(`\n                <!DOCTYPE html>\n                <html>\n                <head>\n                  <title>Quantum Council - Offline</title>\n                  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1">\n                  <style>\n                    body { \n                      font-family: Inter, sans-serif; \n                      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #0a0e27, #1a1f3a);\n                      color: white; \n                      margin: 0; \n                      padding: 40px 20px;\n                      text-align: center;\n                      min-height: 100vh;\n                      display: flex;\n                      flex-direction: column;\n                      justify-content: center;\n                    }\n                    h1 { color: #4A90E2; margin-bottom: 20px; }\n                    p { color: #aaa; max-width: 400px; margin: 0 auto 20px; }\n                    button {\n                      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #4A90E2, #9B59B6);\n                      border: none;\n                      padding: 15px 30px;\n                      border-radius: 10px;\n                      color: white;\n                      font-size: 16px;\n                      cursor: pointer;\n                      margin-top: 20px;\n                    }\n                  </style>\n                </head>\n                <body>\n                  <h1>üåô Quantum Council</h1>\n                  <p>You\'re currently offline. The app is still functional with cached data.</p>\n                  <p>Check your internet connection for the latest features.</p>\n                  <button onclick="window.location.reload()">Try Again</button>\n                </body>\n                </html>\n              `, {\n                headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'text/html\' }\n              });\n            }\n          });\n      })\n  );\n});\n\n// Background sync for data when online\nself.addEventListener(\'sync\', event => {\n  if (event.tag === \'background-sync\') {\n    event.waitUntil(doBackgroundSync());\n  }\n});\n\n// Push notifications (optional future feature)\nself.addEventListener(\'push\', event => {\n  if (event.data) {\n    const data = event.data.json();\n    const options = {\n      body: data.body,\n      icon: \'/icon-192.png\',\n      badge: \'/icon-192.png\',\n      vibrate: [200, 100, 200],\n      data: data.url || \'/\'\n    };\n\n    event.waitUntil(\n      self.registration.showNotification(data.title, options)\n    );\n  }\n});\n\n// Handle notification clicks\nself.addEventListener(\'notificationclick\', event => {\n  event.notification.close();\n  event.waitUntil(\n    clients.openWindow(event.notification.data || \'/\')\n  );\n});\n\nfunction doBackgroundSync() {\n  // This would sync any offline data when the user comes back online\n  console.log(\'[SW] Background sync completed\');\n  return Promise.resolve();\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Add a lightweight daily challenge widget\n\nIn `index.html`, on the Council page (`#council-page`), just under the stats grid, add:\n\n```html\n<div class="card" id="dailyChallengeCard">\n  <div class="card-header">\n    <div>\n      <div class="card-title">\n        <span>üéØ</span>\n        Today\'s Quantum Challenge\n      </div>\n      <div class="card-subtitle" id="dailyChallengeText">\n        Loading challenge...\n      </div>\n    </div>\n    <button class="icon-btn" id="dailyChallengeDoneBtn" onclick="app.completeDailyChallenge()">\n      ‚úÖ\n    </button>\n  </div>\n</div>\n```\n\nIn `app.js`, add a tiny challenge system:\n\n```js\ngetTodayKey() {\n  return new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10); // YYYY-MM-DD\n}\n\ngetDailyChallenge() {\n  const challenges = [\n    "Log one win and one piece of evidence.",\n    "Write down 3 things you\'re grateful for.",\n    "Do a reality check and be brutally honest.",\n    "Spend 2 minutes feeling as if your intention is done.",\n    "Log one synchronicity you notice today."\n  ];\n  const today = this.getTodayKey();\n  // Simple deterministic "random": hash date to index\n  let hash = 0;\n  for (let i = 0; i < today.length; i++) {\n    hash = (hash * 31 + today.charCodeAt(i)) >>> 0;\n  }\n  const index = hash % challenges.length;\n  return challenges[index];\n}\n\nloadCouncilPage() {\n  // existing stats...\n  document.getElementById(\'streakDays\').textContent = this.user.streak;\n  document.getElementById(\'alignmentScore\').textContent = this.calculateAlignment();\n\n  // Daily challenge\n  const challenge = this.getDailyChallenge();\n  document.getElementById(\'dailyChallengeText\').textContent = challenge;\n\n  const completedKey = `challenge_done_${this.getTodayKey()}`;\n  const done = this.storage.get(completedKey);\n  const btn = document.getElementById(\'dailyChallengeDoneBtn\');\n  if (done) {\n    btn.textContent = \'‚úîÔ∏è\';\n    btn.disabled = true;\n    btn.style.opacity = \'0.5\';\n  } else {\n    btn.textContent = \'‚úÖ\';\n    btn.disabled = false;\n    btn.style.opacity = \'1\';\n  }\n\n  // Load messages\n  this.loadMessages();\n}\n\ncompleteDailyChallenge() {\n  const completedKey = `challenge_done_${this.getTodayKey()}`;\n  if (this.storage.get(completedKey)) return;\n\n  this.storage.set(completedKey, true);\n  this.user.points += 10;\n  this.updateUser();\n\n  const btn = document.getElementById(\'dailyChallengeDoneBtn\');\n  if (btn) {\n    btn.textContent = \'‚úîÔ∏è\';\n    btn.disabled = true;\n    btn.style.opacity = \'0.5\';\n  }\n\n  this.showAchievementNotification({\n    name: "Daily Quantum Challenge",\n    description: "You completed today\'s challenge!",\n    points: 10,\n    icon: \'üéØ\'\n  });\n}\n```\n\nThis gives you a **single, focused ‚Äúmission‚Äù for each day** with ~0 extra complexity.\n\n---\n\n## 4.     "Write down 3 things you\'re grateful for.",\n      "Do a reality check and be brutally honest.",\n      "Spend 2 minutes feeling as if your intention is done.",\n      "Log one synchronicity you
